高级软件工程师【我们是谁？】我们是一家做了12年覆盖全球的互联网教育公司。【我们需要谁】1、负责线上绘画课程的基础教学工作，根据教学计划进行课程设计与授课；2、鼓励提升学员学习的自信心，促成学员报名VIP课程；3、热爱教育行业，对教学充满热情，擅长调动课堂气氛；【我们需要什么样的你】1.大专及以上学历，美术相关专业，一年及以上网络游戏行业设计经验优先；2.能够调动课堂气氛，激发学员对原画浓厚的报名兴趣，擅长人际沟通，观察和表达能力强，讲课生动；3.手绘能力好，具有扎实的美术功底，较好的素描造型能力和色彩控制及搭配能力；4.精通 Photoshop、Sai 等设计制作软件；5.语言表达流利，具有一定的演讲和宣传能力；【你关心的待遇】无责底薪5K-10K+业绩提成+五险一金+每天两顿工作餐(只要你能力够强，薪资多少你来定!)月休4天，法定节假日休息；完善的培训体系，专业的带薪培训，全面提升个人能力！【我们有什么】十二年悠久发展历史，总公司+分公司共3000+人规模，领先于同行业的优质资源和广阔平台；高级商务写字楼，环境舒适，靠近地铁站，交通便利；【前途如何】部门领导都是行业老手，姿势多，经验丰富。只要你愿意努力愿意学，毕生绝学全部教教教！舒服 12-6 10:30:42找工作很容易，但找一份能让你坚持做、努力做，当自己的事业来做的工作并不容易。所以，很多人频繁的换工作，却总找不到合适的，却把时间耗在找工作的路上！多年过去，回过头看看，却一事无成…潭州教育，十二年的光辉历程只要你有上进心，你是正能量的人！期待你加入我们的原画讲师！你需要有扎实的美术基础，和良好的美术审美；还要有根据插画，插图需求自行设计二次元，原画美术宣传效果图；并且可以在电脑上，纸上通过视频教学方式教授学员绘画技法。能力要求：1.有良好的手绘能力，擅长线稿表现，色彩表现，更重要的是具备细节刻画的能力；2.擅长画动漫二次元，游戏动漫；3.能够根据课程大纲，设计绘画教程；个人简历需附带个人美术作品，如无作品，概不回复

算法工程师Test Development Engineer     Job Description    Candidate will be part of Product  Operations team supporting high-end switch product line. This is core business  area for Cisco supported by high investments and a robust roadmap. This  position offers excellent learning and career development opportunities both on  the technology and leadership. Candidate should expect a fast-paced environment  and close collaboration with global cross functional team. Qualified Candidate  will expect to take following responsibility:    ·        Reports to Manager of ProdOps, interfaces  with MFG Engineering and Design Engineering functions on a regular basis  regarding technical issues, testability, and MFG test strategy. Develop MFG  test plan and capital investment plan, host test plan review and  approval.     ·        Interacts with contract manufacture test  team for test plan execution and test deployment. Order and construct test  equipment per approved test plan. Develop and validate test scripts.    ·        Review Diagnostic test coverage with  design engineer, and develop test and diagnostic programs.    ·        Solve Test and DFT issues and provide  feedback to NPI groups.    ·        Design, procure, and build test fixtures  and equipment for production test use.    ·        Being part of agile NPI team, receive  minimal direction toward daily goals and objectives. Work is reviewed and  measured based on attainment of overall objectives and success of product  metrics.    ·        Support prototype build, take leadership  in driving manufacture test failure analysis and corrective action. Respond to  production test related problems by working with Production TE, supplier and  Design Engineering as required.    ·        Generates documentation for test coverage  analysis, test platform/application development, and on specific capital  equipment required by production testing.    Desired Skills and Qualification    ·        Motivated individual with BSEE, or BSCE or  equivalent.    ·        Minimum 3 years of manufacture test or HW  validation experience, experience in HW or diagnostics development highly  preferred.    ·        Ability to design and execute development  projects with a design of experiment approach (DOE) to service, troubleshoot,  and solve engineering problems.    ·        Experienced in working with global team.  Strong interpersonal and team skills, good presentation skills for cross  functional communications    ·        Fluent in English and Mandarin.    ·        Experienced with NPI processes and  manufacturing environment.    ·        Knowledge and experience with Ethernet  switching or routing products    ·        Experienced in HW troubleshooting at PCBA  level    ·        Experienced in software programming using  C/C++ and/or scripting language. Python experience is highly preferred.    ·        Test automation platform such as Labview  is a plus.    ·        Experienced in L2 and L3 traffic test with  traffic generator such as IXIA, Spirent, etc.

Your work will include but not limited as follow:1.Work closely with PO and team to research test solution and develop new functionalities to fulfill product design and testing needs.2.Continuously improve test framework from architecture and solution level.3.Research and bring mainstream open source technology from internet industry to fulfill development and improvement needs.4.Collect feedback from product developers and promote new functionalities to targets users.5.Troubleshooting and bug fixQualifications:1.Self-motivated, team player and passionate for quality2.Eager to learn and practice new technology3.Open mind, positive attitude4.Innovative and solution thinking ability5.Good English communication in both written and spokenExperience/knowledge within the following areas is required:1.Proficient work experience on Linux/Unix system2.Good understanding of computer science knowledge, including Operating System, IP network and protocols such as TCP/UDP3.Following script languages: Strong Python, basic Shell and basic Perl4.Familiar with GitExperience/knowledge within the following areas is a plus:

软件测试SSD Firmware Testing Execution(固态硬盘嵌入式固件测试执行) Description:  Exciting opportunities awaits you at Micron’s fast growing Shanghai SSD test execution team. As a SSD (Solid State Drive) Firmware Testing Execution (固件测试工程师/嵌入式软件测试执行) in Micron’s MSD group, you will work with an exceptionally talented core team based in Shanghai, to test and verify controller firmware for NAND-based mass storage solutions in the consumer and enterprise segments. You will also have the opportunity to work closely with fellow US based firmware engineers, system hardware design engineers, product engineers, and Flash memory design engineers, to solve cross-functional design issues.  Your main responsibilities will include: find bugs through white and black box testing; execute test script to validate the product’s functional specifications behavior; report detected bugs and update report to project team; build up SSD test environment and being able to check and fix environment issues; develop simple script/tool to improve working efficiency.    Qualifications:  Successful candidates for this position will have:  - At least one years or equivalent experience in software or firmware testing.  - Experience on script/tool development with python/shell script language is a plus. - Fluent English writing and speaking. - Meticulous and attention to details, patience and passion, strive to ensure maximum test cases coverage.  - Clear headed, goal oriented, systematic and methodical approach in software testing - Ability to enter clear and concise documentation is a must.  - Ability to work and communicate effectively in a team, able to multitask effectively in fast-paced environment.  - Knowledge of mass storage systems (hard disk), Flash memory (NAND / NOR), and device drivers (optional but strong plus).  - Experience in automation test framework such as Jenkins, Robot (optional but strong plus).  - Knowledge of mass storage interfaces such as ATA, SATA, and/or SAS/FC (optional but strong plus).  - Knowledge of SSD flash translation layer, wear leveling, garbage collection (optional but strong plus).  - Experience in test equipment such as oscilloscopes and logic/bus analyzers (optional but plus).   Education:  BS in Electrical / Computer Engineering or Computer Science is preferred

其他【项目介绍】   数据人才培养计划”是亚信科技（中国）有限公司产品研发交付中心发起，由CTO亲自带领，数据科学技术专家支持，在研发体系最核心的部门，面对高端数据人才--“未来科学家”开展的专项培养计划。   在“数据人才培养计划”中，亚信科技将继续秉承自身研发体系里学术与产品化并重的优势，创建自己的数据科学研究院和实验室，专注于人工智能、机器学习、云计算、大数据技术在移动通信网络、移动互联网、5G等领域的应用。   亚信科技鼓励“未来科学家”们进行学术创新，专注于新领域的技术研究、发表论文、申请专利，并提供参加国际学术会议、行业会议的机会。    【工作职责】   1、在移动通信和移动互联网领域，利用数据科学专业知识进行通信与互联网机器学习，人工智能等相关产品的研发工作；  2、运用量化分析、数据挖掘和数据可视化方面的专业知识，为我们提供超越数字层面的专业洞察；   3、运用数据和业务规则解决大规模网络中系统和数据基础架构中潜在的问题；4、在跨功能域/跨职能部门的工作中定义问题陈述，收集数据，构建分析模型并提出建议；  5、构建和维护数据驱动的优化模型，实验，预测算法和容量约束模型；6、建立分析模型来识别和输出推动网络系统关键决策；7、能熟练运用R，Python, Spark, Hadoop和SQL, Tableau等工具来提高分析效率；  8、通过探索性分析以发现新机遇：了解移动通信和互联网生态系统，用户行为和长期趋势。【职位要求】   1、计算机、通信与信息工程、数学、统计、电子工程、物理等相关专业的博士或优秀的硕士；   2、熟练掌握至少2种语言：Python, R, Matlab, SQL, Scala, Spark, PHP, SAS, Weka等；   3、拥有优秀的统计知识；   4、对移动通信或互联网行业知识有一定了解，包括移动互联网行业、手机制造商、通信网络设备供应商和/或芯片组供应商等；   5、能与产品和领导团队流畅沟通分析结果，以讨论并影响产品战略的制定；   6、有在国内外知名期刊或会议（SCI/EI检索）有通信、计算机或数据科学领域相关论文发表；   7、具备较强的英文科研文献阅读与撰写能力。大学英语六级/或托福、雅思。
